#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x063D [0x32] ExtData[1]->MainSpeed = 13* * 0.1
  1: 0x0640 [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: EventEntity moves to X=-19.713*, Z=-105.623*, Y=-4.000*
  2: 0x0648 [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: Update entity position (mode=1)
  3: 0x064A [0x6F] WAIT_FRAME_DELAY: Yield until WaitTime reaches zero
  4: 0x064B [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
